***север.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:север.html>север</a> (1938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sěverъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱeh₁wero</i>. Cognate with Lithuanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="li">šiaurė</i>, Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caurus</i> and English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shower</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:север.html>се́вер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">séver</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:север.html>се́вера</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>north</li>
<li>North <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">northern part of any region</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>Arctic <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">northern parts of Russia</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крайний.html>кра́йний</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:север.html>се́вер</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Krájnij <b>Séver</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Far North <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Russian territories that lie to the north of the Arctic circle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>се́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вера.html>ве́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">сѣверный</span>)
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***сегодня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> (235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сего</a> дьне</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sego dĭne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*se dьne</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sego dьne</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">this</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьnь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sej</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of this</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">denʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sevódnja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>today
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тром</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sevódnja</b> útrom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this morning</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sevódnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>today, this day</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седой.html>седо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sedój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седеть.html>седе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sedétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поседеть.html>поседе́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:седловина.html>седлови́на</a> (16963)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седловина.html>седлови́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sedlovína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седловина.html>седлови́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седловина.html>седлови́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седловина.html>седлови́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> saddleback, saddle, col</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:седловина.html>седлови́на</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:седой.html>седо́й</a> (1819)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:седой.html>седо́й</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***седьмой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьмо́й</a> (2169)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">седьмъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sedĭmŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">седмъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sedmŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">семъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">semŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sedmъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seventh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sebdmъ</i> lt; <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*septmъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*septmas</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*septmós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьмо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sedʹmój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>seventh</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьмо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sedʹmój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьма́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sedʹmája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

***сей.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a> (602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">this</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sej</span>) (<i>demonstrative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> this, this here
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочитать.html>прочита́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нт</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упоминаться.html>упомина́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоимость.html>сто́имость</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pročitál ja <b>sej</b> dokumént, nu i gde tam upominájetsja stóimostʹ?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I've read this document, well, where is the cost mentioned there?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>Сей</a></b> is an archaic form that is seldom used in speech or in prose unless compounded with other words or in certain set phrases:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sevódnja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">today</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sejčás</i> ― <span class="e-translation">immediately</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сию́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sijú minútu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this very minute</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>по́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do six pór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">until now</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po sej denʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">until this day</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri sjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">herewith</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i tó i sjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">both this and the other</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">to da sjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one thing and another</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni tó ni sjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">neither the one nor the other</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li>It can also be used in a stilted or jocular style.</li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sej</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">second-person singular imperative imperfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">séjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:указательный.html>Указа́тельное</a> местоимение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — lt;2bgt;.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:образовать.html>Образу́ет</a> омоформы <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>се́ю</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> гл. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a></i>.

***сейчас.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> (98)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sej</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ”this hour”, ”this time” (note: “сей” is dated, bookish or stilted (unlike “э́тот”), “час” in the sense of “time” is dated or poetic).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sejčás</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>now, at present</li>
<li>presently, immediately, at once</li>
<li>just now</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tepérʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>ча́с</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, обстоятельственное, <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>; неизменяемое.

***секвестр.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:секвестр.html>секве́стр</a> (31991)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sekwestr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sequestrum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sequester</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sequester</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">intermediary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sequester</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секвестр.html>секве́стр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sekvéstr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секвестр.html>секве́стра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секвестр.html>секве́стры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секвестр.html>секве́стров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sequestration
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накладывать.html>накла́дывать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:секвестр.html>секве́стр</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nakládyvatʹ <b>sekvéstr</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sequestrate; sequester</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sequestrum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sequester, across-the-board cut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:секвестр.html>секве́стр</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бюджет.html>бюдже́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sekvéstr</b> bjudžéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(state) budget sequester</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:секира.html>секи́ра</a> (13914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sekyra</i>, related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sečʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секира.html>секи́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sekíra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секира.html>секи́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секира.html>секи́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секира.html>секи́р</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:секретарша.html>секрета́рша</a> (4494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секретарь.html>секрета́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sekretárʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секретарша.html>секрета́рша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sekretárša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секретарша.html>секрета́рши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секретарша.html>секрета́рши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секретарша.html>секрета́рш</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:секретарь.html>секрета́рь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> secretary <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">female</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the wife of a secretary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коллежский.html>колле́жская</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:секретарша.html>секрета́рша</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kolléžskaja <b>sekretárša</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <b>wife of the</b> collegiate <b>secretary</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Some occupation names work for both males and females. The male form of the term may refer to a male or a female. This is a more colloquial term and is likely to be negatively perceived.</li></ul>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sekretär</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sekretarz</i>.
